{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_019s4WjhMHQxXnh8uLkUtC1F","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_013CJQn19LXfKn9NYd2uUeTk","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/RELEASE_NOTES.md","content":"# Flipt Release Notes\n\nThis document summarizes the API changes in Flipt v1.40.0 and v1.40.1, focusing on breaking changes, new features, deprecations, and upgrade guidance.\n\n---\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n> These changes require action from users upgrading.\n\n**Note:** This release maintains backward compatibility for most APIs. Deprecated fields continue to work but should be migrated to their replacements.\n\n- **[gRPC API]**: The primary `Evaluate` and `BatchEvaluate` RPC methods in the main `Flipt` service are now deprecated in favor of the new `EvaluationService`. While the old methods remain functional, new implementations should use the evaluation service.\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### Evaluation Service API (Separated from Main Service)\n\nThe evaluation API has been refactored into a dedicated `EvaluationService` with improved request/response types:\n\n**New Endpoints:**\n- `rpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse)` — Evaluate boolean flags\n- `rpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns (VariantEvaluationResponse)` — Evaluate variant flags\n- `rpc Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest) returns (BatchEvaluationResponse)` — Batch evaluate multiple flags\n\n**New Response Structure:**\n- `BooleanEvaluationResponse`: Simplified response for boolean flag evaluation with reason codes\n- `VariantEvaluationResponse`: Variant evaluation response with reason and attachment support\n- `ErrorEvaluationResponse`: Dedicated error response type\n\n**Example (gRPC/Protobuf):**\n```protobuf\nservice EvaluationService {\n  rpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse) {}\n  rpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns (VariantEvaluationResponse) {}\n  rpc Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest) returns (BatchEvaluationResponse) {}\n}\n\nmessage EvaluationRequest {\n  string request_id = 1;\n  string namespace_key = 2;\n  string flag_key = 3;\n  string entity_id = 4;\n  map<string, string> context = 5;\n  string reference = 6;\n}\n\nmessage BooleanEvaluationResponse {\n  bool enabled = 1;\n  EvaluationReason reason = 2;\n  string request_id = 3;\n  double request_duration_millis = 4;\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp timestamp = 5;\n  string flag_key = 6;\n}\n```\n\n### Multi-Segment Support in Rules and Rollouts\n\nRules and rollouts now support multiple segments with logical operators (AND/OR):\n\n**New Fields:**\n- `Rule.segment_keys` (repeated) — Multiple segments for rule matching\n- `Rule.segment_operator` — Operator type (OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR=0, AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR=1)\n- `RolloutSegment.segment_keys` (repeated) — Multiple segments for rollout evaluation\n- `RolloutSegment.segment_operator` — Operator for segment matching\n\n**Request Types Updated:**\n- `CreateRuleRequest.segment_keys` + `segment_operator`\n- `UpdateRuleRequest.segment_keys` + `segment_operator`\n- `CreateRolloutRequest.segment_keys` (in RolloutSegment)\n- `UpdateRolloutRequest.segment_keys` (in RolloutSegment)\n\n### OCI Storage Integration with AWS ECR\n\nEnhanced OCI storage backend with better AWS ECR integration:\n\n**New Configuration Options:**\n- Configurable OCI manifest version support for better ECR compatibility (#2941)\n\n**REST API Support:**\n- Storage configuration now accepts manifest version specifications for OCI-compatible registries\n\n### File System Storage with Git Integration\n\nAdded directory scope support for Git-based file system storage:\n\n**New Features:**\n- Configure a specific directory scope for file system storage backends (#2939)\n- Useful for monorepo setups or scoped feature flag configuration\n\n### Flipt Validate Command Enhancements\n\nCLI validation tool now supports working directory specification:\n\n**REST API:**\n- New `--working-directory` parameter for `flipt validate` command (#2936)\n- Allows validation of configuration files relative to a specific directory\n\n### GitHub Authentication Enhancements\n\nGitHub authentication method now supports team membership verification:\n\n**New Capability:**\n- Team membership check integrated into GitHub authentication flow (#2891)\n- Enables organization and team-based access control\n\n### Redis Cache Username Support\n\nRedis cache configuration now accepts username credentials:\n\n**New Configuration:**\n- `cache.redis` configuration now supports `username` parameter (#2953)\n- Supports Redis 6.0+ ACL authentication\n\n---\n\n## Deprecations\n\n> Deprecated features remain functional but should be migrated to their replacements.\n\n### API Pagination: `offset` → `page_token`\n\n**Since:** v1.13.0\n\n`offset` parameter is deprecated in favor of cursor-based pagination.\n\n**Affected List Operations:**\n- `ListFlagRequest` — Use `page_token` instead of `offset`\n- `ListSegmentRequest` — Use `page_token` instead of `offset`\n- `ListRuleRequest` — Use `page_token` instead of `offset`\n- `ListNamespaceRequest` — Use `page_token` instead of `offset`\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. Replace `offset` integer with `page_token` string\n2. Use `next_page_token` from previous response for subsequent pages\n3. Set `limit` to control result size (works with both approaches)\n\n**Example:**\n```protobuf\n// Before (deprecated)\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  int32 limit = 1;\n  int32 offset = 2 [deprecated = true];  // Don't use\n  string namespace_key = 4;\n}\n\n// After (recommended)\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  int32 limit = 1;\n  string page_token = 3;  // Use this\n  string namespace_key = 4;\n}\n\nmessage FlagList {\n  repeated Flag flags = 1;\n  string next_page_token = 2;  // Pass this for next request\n  int32 total_count = 3;\n}\n```\n\n### Single Segment Fields → Multiple Segments\n\n**Since:** Various versions (v1.39.0+)\n\nSingle `segment_key` fields are deprecated in favor of repeated `segment_keys` with logical operators.\n\n**Deprecated Fields:**\n- `Rule.segment_key` — Use `Rule.segment_keys` + `segment_operator`\n- `CreateRuleRequest.segment_key` — Use `segment_keys` + `segment_operator`\n- `UpdateRuleRequest.segment_key` — Use `segment_keys` + `segment_operator`\n- `RolloutSegment.segment_key` — Use `segment_keys` + `segment_operator`\n- `EvaluationResponse.segment_key` — Use `segment_keys` (array)\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. For single segment rules: Move value to `segment_keys[0]` and set `segment_operator = OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR`\n2. For multiple segments: Add all segment keys to `segment_keys` array\n3. Choose operator: `OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR` if any segment matches, `AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR` if all must match\n\n**Example:**\n```protobuf\n// Before (deprecated)\nmessage CreateRuleRequest {\n  string flag_key = 1;\n  string segment_key = 2 [deprecated = true];  // Don't use\n  int32 rank = 3;\n}\n\n// After (recommended)\nmessage CreateRuleRequest {\n  string flag_key = 1;\n  repeated string segment_keys = 5;  // Use this\n  SegmentOperator segment_operator = 6;  // AND or OR\n}\n\nenum SegmentOperator {\n  OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR = 0;      // Match if ANY segment matches\n  AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR = 1;     // Match if ALL segments match\n}\n```\n\n### Deprecated gRPC Evaluation Methods\n\n**Since:** v1.40.0\n\nMain service evaluation methods are deprecated:\n- `Flipt.Evaluate()` — Use `EvaluationService.Variant()`\n- `Flipt.BatchEvaluate()` — Use `EvaluationService.Batch()`\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. Use new `EvaluationService` for evaluation requests\n2. Response structures have changed (see New Features section)\n3. Old methods continue to work but won't receive new features\n\n**Removal Timeline:** ~1 year from v1.40.0 (approximately April 2025)\n\n### Jaeger Tracing Exporter\n\n**Since:** v1.36.0 | **Removed in:** v1.36.0+\n\nJaeger exporter is no longer supported. OpenTelemetry dropped Jaeger support.\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. Switch to OTLP (OpenTelemetry Protocol) exporter\n2. Configure `tracing.exporter: otlp` instead of `jaeger`\n3. Update collector endpoint to OTLP-compatible receiver\n\n**Configuration Example:**\n```yaml\n# Before (no longer works)\ntracing:\n  exporter: jaeger\n  jaeger:\n    endpoint: http://localhost:14268/api/traces\n\n# After (current)\ntracing:\n  exporter: otlp\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: http://localhost:4317\n```\n\n### Authentication Metadata Exclusion\n\n**Since:** Recently deprecated (not yet in old version)\n\nConfiguration option `authentication.exclude.metadata` is deprecated.\n\n**Reason:** Feature never worked as intended. Metadata cannot be excluded from authentication when required.\n\n**Action:** Remove this configuration option — metadata is always included when authentication is enabled.\n\n---\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\n### v1.40.1\n\n- **Authentication**: Fixed auth hash caching to only store hash, not plaintext (#2974)\n- **Authentication**: Skip database connection when not necessary (#2973)\n- **Cache**: Added username support in Redis configuration (#2953)\n\n### v1.40.0\n\n- **Evaluator**: No longer errors on parsing failures (#2918)\n- **Validation**: JSON schema now correctly validates `key|keys` in rollout segments (#2947)\n- **Tracing**: Fixed invalid trace log level schema (#2946)\n- **UI**: Evaluation console now warns users about required context values (#2937)\n- **Segment**: Fixed segment constraint isolation issue across namespaces (#2920)\n- **Evaluator**: Fixed IsNotOneOf operator using incorrect logic (#2912)\n\n---\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\n### For Users on v1.39.x or Earlier\n\n#### Step 1: Backup Configuration and Data\n\n```bash\n# Backup your flipt configuration\ncp -r ~/.flipt ~/.flipt.backup\n\n# Backup your database (adjust path for your storage backend)\ncp flipt.db flipt.db.backup\n```\n\n#### Step 2: Stop Flipt\n\n```bash\n# Stop your running Flipt instance\nsystemctl stop flipt\n# or\ndocker stop flipt\n```\n\n#### Step 3: Upgrade Binary\n\n**Docker:**\n```bash\ndocker pull markphelps/flipt:v1.40.1\n```\n\n**Binary:**\n```bash\n# Download from https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/releases/tag/v1.40.1\nflipt version  # Verify upgrade\n```\n\n**macOS (Homebrew):**\n```bash\nbrew upgrade flipt\n```\n\n#### Step 4: Update API Client Code\n\n**If using pagination (offset-based):**\n\nReplace offset-based pagination:\n```python\n# Before\nresponse = flipt_client.list_flags(namespace_key=\"default\", offset=0, limit=10)\n\n# After\nresponse = flipt_client.list_flags(namespace_key=\"default\", limit=10)\npage_token = response.next_page_token\nresponse = flipt_client.list_flags(namespace_key=\"default\", page_token=page_token, limit=10)\n```\n\n**If using evaluation API:**\n\nUpdate gRPC calls to use new EvaluationService:\n```go\n// Before (deprecated, but still works)\nresp, err := client.Evaluate(ctx, &flipt.EvaluationRequest{\n    RequestId: \"req-1\",\n    FlagKey: \"my-flag\",\n    EntityId: \"user-123\",\n})\n\n// After (recommended)\nresp, err := evaluationClient.Variant(ctx, &evaluation.EvaluationRequest{\n    RequestId: \"req-1\",\n    FlagKey: \"my-flag\",\n    EntityId: \"user-123\",\n})\n```\n\n**If using single segment rules:**\n\nUpdate to multi-segment format:\n```protobuf\n// Before (deprecated)\nCreateRuleRequest {\n  segment_key: \"beta-users\"\n}\n\n// After (recommended)\nCreateRuleRequest {\n  segment_keys: [\"beta-users\"]\n  segment_operator: OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\n}\n```\n\n#### Step 5: Test Configuration\n\nValidate your configuration file:\n```bash\nflipt validate --config-file /path/to/flipt.yml\n```\n\n#### Step 6: Start Flipt\n\n```bash\n# Start your Flipt instance\nsystemctl start flipt\n# or\ndocker start flipt\n```\n\n#### Step 7: Verify Functionality\n\n```bash\n# Test evaluation API\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:8080/api/v1/evaluate \\\n  -H \"Content-Type: application/json\" \\\n  -d '{\n    \"flag_key\": \"test-flag\",\n    \"entity_id\": \"user-1\",\n    \"namespace_key\": \"default\"\n  }'\n\n# Test gRPC health\ngrpcurl -plaintext localhost:50051 list\n```\n\n### For Users with Custom Deployments\n\n**Redis Cache Configuration:**\n\nIf using Redis cache with authentication, add username:\n\n```yaml\n# Before\ncache:\n  redis:\n    host: redis-server\n    password: your-password\n\n# After (with v6.0+ ACL)\ncache:\n  redis:\n    host: redis-server\n    username: default\n    password: your-password\n```\n\n**OCI Storage with AWS ECR:**\n\nIf using OCI storage, you may now configure manifest version:\n\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  type: oci\n  oci:\n    repository: my-aws-account.dkr.ecr.region.amazonaws.com/flipt\n    manifest_version: v2  # New option for ECR compatibility\n```\n\n**File System Storage with Git:**\n\nNew directory scope for git-based storage:\n\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  type: git\n  git:\n    repository: https://github.com/org/flags\n    directory: /flags  # New: scope to specific directory\n```\n\n**GitHub Authentication:**\n\nTeam membership is now checked. Ensure your OAuth app has appropriate scopes:\n\n```yaml\nauthentication:\n  methods:\n    github:\n      enabled: true\n      client_id: your-client-id\n      client_secret: your-client-secret\n      # Optional: require team membership\n      # team_slugs: [org/platform-team]\n```\n\n### Rollback Instructions\n\nIf you encounter issues:\n\n```bash\n# Stop the new version\nsystemctl stop flipt\n\n# Restore from backup\ncp -r ~/.flipt.backup ~/.flipt\n\n# Restore binary from package manager or previous release\napt-get install flipt=1.39.0  # Replace with your previous version\n\n# Start the previous version\nsystemctl start flipt\n```\n\n---\n\n## API Reference Summary\n\n### New EvaluationService Endpoints\n\n| Method | Request Type | Response Type | Purpose |\n|--------|--------------|---------------|---------|\n| `Boolean` | `EvaluationRequest` | `BooleanEvaluationResponse` | Evaluate boolean flags |\n| `Variant` | `EvaluationRequest` | `VariantEvaluationResponse` | Evaluate variant flags |\n| `Batch` | `BatchEvaluationRequest` | `BatchEvaluationResponse` | Batch evaluation |\n| `EvaluationSnapshotNamespace` | `EvaluationNamespaceSnapshotRequest` | `EvaluationNamespaceSnapshot` | Get namespace snapshot for evaluation |\n\n### List Endpoints Using Page Token\n\nAll list endpoints now support cursor-based pagination:\n- `ListFlags(ListFlagRequest) → FlagList`\n- `ListSegments(ListSegmentRequest) → SegmentList`\n- `ListRules(ListRuleRequest) → RuleList`\n- `ListNamespaces(ListNamespaceRequest) → NamespaceList`\n- `ListRollouts(ListRolloutRequest) → RolloutList`\n\n---\n\n## Support\n\n- **Documentation**: https://docs.flipt.io\n- **Issues**: https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/issues\n- **Discussions**: https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/discussions\n- **Deprecation Policy**: See `DEPRECATIONS.md` in the repository\n\n---\n\n## Version Information\n\n- **Latest Release**: v1.40.1 (2024-04-11)\n- **Previous Release**: v1.40.0 (2024-04-05)\n- **Release Date**: April 2024\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1007,"cache_read_input_tokens":60045,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1007},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e3652277-b373-4933-94fc-43a93eb1746c","uuid":"5ae0a439-62d7-4c70-8d3c-1be29eca2de0"}

Deprecated fields continue to work but should be migrated to their replacements.\n\n- **[gRPC API]**: The primary `Evaluate` and `BatchEvaluate` RPC methods in the main `Flipt` service are now deprecated in favor of the new `EvaluationService`. While the old methods remain functional, new implementations should use the evaluation service.\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### Evaluation Service API (Separated from Main Service)\n\nThe evaluation API has been refactored into a dedicated `EvaluationService` with improved request/response types:\n\n**New Endpoints:**\n- `rpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse)` — Evaluate boolean flags\n- `rpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns (VariantEvaluationResponse)` — Evaluate variant flags\n- `rpc Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest) returns (BatchEvaluationResponse)` — Batch evaluate multiple flags\n\n**New Response Structure:**\n- `BooleanEvaluationResponse`: Simplified response for boolean flag evaluation with reason codes\n- `VariantEvaluationResponse`: Variant evaluation response with reason and attachment support\n- `ErrorEvaluationResponse`: Dedicated error response type\n\n**Example (gRPC/Protobuf):**\n```protobuf\nservice EvaluationService {\n  rpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse) {}\n  rpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns (VariantEvaluationResponse) {}\n  rpc Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest) returns (BatchEvaluationResponse) {}\n}\n\nmessage EvaluationRequest {\n  string request_id = 1;\n  string namespace_key = 2;\n  string flag_key = 3;\n  string entity_id = 4;\n  map<string, string> context = 5;\n  string reference = 6;\n}\n\nmessage BooleanEvaluationResponse {\n  bool enabled = 1;\n  EvaluationReason reason = 2;\n  string request_id = 3;\n  double request_duration_millis = 4;\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp timestamp = 5;\n  string flag_key = 6;\n}\n```\n\n### Multi-Segment Support in Rules and Rollouts\n\nRules and rollouts now support multiple segments with logical operators (AND/OR):\n\n**New Fields:**\n- `Rule.segment_keys` (repeated) — Multiple segments for rule matching\n- `Rule.segment_operator` — Operator type (OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR=0, AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR=1)\n- `RolloutSegment.segment_keys` (repeated) — Multiple segments for rollout evaluation\n- `RolloutSegment.segment_operator` — Operator for segment matching\n\n**Request Types Updated:**\n- `CreateRuleRequest.segment_keys` + `segment_operator`\n- `UpdateRuleRequest.segment_keys` + `segment_operator`\n- `CreateRolloutRequest.segment_keys` (in RolloutSegment)\n- `UpdateRolloutRequest.segment_keys` (in RolloutSegment)\n\n### OCI Storage Integration with AWS ECR\n\nEnhanced OCI storage backend with better AWS ECR integration:\n\n**New Configuration Options:**\n- Configurable OCI manifest version support for better ECR compatibility (#2941)\n\n**REST API Support:**\n- Storage configuration now accepts manifest version specifications for OCI-compatible registries\n\n### File System Storage with Git Integration\n\nAdded directory scope support for Git-based file system storage:\n\n**New Features:**\n- Configure a specific directory scope for file system storage backends (#2939)\n- Useful for monorepo setups or scoped feature flag configuration\n\n### Flipt Validate Command Enhancements\n\nCLI validation tool now supports working directory specification:\n\n**REST API:**\n- New `--working-directory` parameter for `flipt validate` command (#2936)\n- Allows validation of configuration files relative to a specific directory\n\n### GitHub Authentication Enhancements\n\nGitHub authentication method now supports team membership verification:\n\n**New Capability:**\n- Team membership check integrated into GitHub authentication flow (#2891)\n- Enables organization and team-based access control\n\n### Redis Cache Username Support\n\nRedis cache configuration now accepts username credentials:\n\n**New Configuration:**\n- `cache.redis` configuration now supports `username` parameter (#2953)\n- Supports Redis 6.0+ ACL authentication\n\n---\n\n## Deprecations\n\n> Deprecated features remain functional but should be migrated to their replacements.\n\n### API Pagination: `offset` → `page_token`\n\n**Since:** v1.13.0\n\n`offset` parameter is deprecated in favor of cursor-based pagination.\n\n**Affected List Operations:**\n- `ListFlagRequest` — Use `page_token` instead of `offset`\n- `ListSegmentRequest` — Use `page_token` instead of `offset`\n- `ListRuleRequest` — Use `page_token` instead of `offset`\n- `ListNamespaceRequest` — Use `page_token` instead of `offset`\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1.
